$~NYAÑN~FUSUNUNÑYAR¿S¿NDANÑFAZLAS¿N¿NÑÎEHIRLERDEÑYAÎAMAYAÑ               Today, more than half of world’s population lives in cities and
BAÎLAD¿Ë¿ÑVEÑ£ÎEHIRLIÑBINY¿L¤ÑOLARAKÑAN¿LMAYAÑBAÎLAYANÑG~N~M~ZÑ          our era is referred to as the “urban millenium”; under these
KOÎULLAR¿NDAÑB~Y~KÑÎEHIRLERINÑHALIHAZ¿RDAÑTAÎ¿D¿KLAR¿ÑDOËALÑ            circumstances, the existing natural risks emanating from the
TEHLIKELEREÑYyNELIKÑRISKLERÑGIDEREKÑART¿YORÑ                            cities are increasing.

eLKEMIZINÑENÑB~Y~KÑMETROPOL~ÑOLANÑÌSTANBULÑISEÑSAHIPÑOLDUËUÑVEÑ          Istanbul, as the biggest city in Turkey, on the one hand protects
~RETTIËIÑDEËERLERLEÑBIRÑYANDANÑ~LKENINÑK~LT~RÑEKONOMIÑVEÑSANAYIÑ        its position as the cultural, economical and industrial center of
MERKEZIÑOLMAÑyZELLIËINIÑKORURKENÑyTEÑYANDANÑ+UZEYÑ!NADOLUÑ&AYÑ          the country with its natural and produced values and on the
(ATT¿¦NAÑYAK¿NÑKONUMUÑNEDENIÑILEÑY~KSEKÑDEPREMÑRISKIÑTAÎ¿YORÑ           other hand, it bears a high earthquake risk due to its location
ÌSTANBUL¦DAÑYAÎANABILECEKÑBIRÑDEPREMÑKENTINÑSADECEÑKENDISINIÑ           near the North Anatolian Fault Line. A possible earthquake in
DEËILÑEKONOMIKÑOLARAKÑB~T~NÑ~LKEYIÑETKILEMEÑPOTANSIYELIÑTAÎ¿YOR        Istanbul has the potential to affect not only the city itself, but
                                                                         also the whole country economically.
ÌSTANBULÑCOËRAFIÑKONUMUÑN~FUSUÑYERLEÎMEÑALANLAR¿N¿NÑKULLAN¿M¿Ñ
SOSYALÑYAP¿S¿ÑVEÑ~LKEÑEKONOMISIÑIlINDEÑTAÎ¿D¿Ë¿ÑyNEMÑGIBIÑNEDENLERÑ      For several reasons such as its geographical location,
DOLAY¿S¿YLAÑDEPREMÑBAÎTAÑOLMAKÑ~ZEREÑlEÎITLIÑAFETÑRISKLERIÑILEÑKARÎ¿Ñ   population, utilization of the residential areas, social structure
KARÎ¿YAÑ                                                                and its significance for the economy of the country, Istanbul
                                                                         would be affected severely by disasters like earthquakes.
!RAÎT¿RMALARÑÌSTANBUL¦DAÑYAÎANABILECEKÑBIRÑDEPREMINÑCANÑVEÑMALÑ
KAY¿PLAR¿ÑILEÑBIRLIKTEÑCIDDIÑEKONOMIKÑSOSYALÑVEÑlEVRESELÑETKILEREÑDEÑ   Researches show that an earthquake which could occur in
YOLÑAlACAË¿N¿ÑGySTERIYORÑ"AZ¿ÑKAYNAKLARAÑGyREÑByYLEÑBIRÑFELAKETINÑ     Istanbul will not only cause mortality and anguish, but will have
ÑMILYARÑDOLARDANÑDAHAÑY~KSEKÑBIRÑEKONOMIKÑETKIYEÑSAHIPÑ                serious economic, social and environmental impacts. According
OLACAË¿ÑTAHMINÑEDILIYORÑ"UG~NÑ~LKEMIZDEÑVEÑÌSTANBUL¦DAÑYAÎANANÑ         to some sources, such a disaster is likely to have an economical
AFETLERDENÑAL¿NANÑDERSLERÑVEÑULUSLARARAS¿ÑGELIÎMELERÑDOËRULTUSUNDAÑ      impact of over 50 billion USD. Significant progress has been
HAYATAÑGElIRILENÑUYGULAMALARDAÑyNEMLIÑMESAFELERÑKATEDILDIÑ              made in practices realized in parallel with the lessons learnt
                                                                         from the past disasters in Istanbul and with international
                                                                         developments.
!FETLERÑOLUÎMADANÑyNCEÑyNLEMÑALMAÑFAALIYETLERINIÑIlERENÑ£RISKÑ       “Risk mitigation” and “preparedness” activities, which include
AZALTMA¤ÑVEÑ£HAZ¿RL¿KL¿ÑOLMA¤ÑlAL¿ÎMALAR¿ÑAFETÑYyNETIMIÑ             taking precautions before disasters happen, have become the
UYGULAMALAR¿N¿NÑENÑyNEMLIÑBILEÎENIÑHALINEÑGELDIÑÌSTANBUL¦UNÑ         most important component of disaster management practices.
DEPREMÑBAÎTAÑOLMAKÑ~ZEREÑYAÎANABILECEKÑAFETLEREÑKARÎ¿ÑHAZ¿RL¿KL¿Ñ     One of the projects actualized in order to prepare the city of
OLMAS¿N¿ÑSAËLAMAKÑAMAC¿YLAÑHAYATAÑGElIRILENÑPROJELERDENÑBIRIÑDEÑ      Istanbul and its citizens for a disaster, primarily an earthquake,
Ì3-%0¦TIR                                                            is Istanbul Seismic Risk Mitigation and Emergency Preparedness
                                                                      Project (ISMEP).
Ì3-%0ÑAFETÑyNCESIÑAFETÑZAMAN¿ÑVEÑSONRAS¿ÑIlINÑGEREKLIÑOLANÑ
HAZ¿RL¿KÑZARARÑAZALTMAÑM~DAHALEÑVEÑIYILEÎTIRMEYEÑYyNELIKÑ           ISMEP is a comprehensive project which covers supportive and
DESTEKLEYICIÑVEÑyNLEYICIÑUYGULAMALAR¿ÑELEÑALANÑGENIÎÑKAPSAML¿ÑBIRÑ    preventive practices directed towards preparedness, mitigation,
lAL¿ÎMAÑ0ROJEÑBIREYÑAILEÑVEÑKURUMSALÑD~ZEYDEÑRISKÑAZALT¿C¿Ñ        response and recovery including the periods before, during and
yNLEMLERLEÑyZELLIKLEÑDEPREMLERDENÑKAYNAKLANANÑACILÑDURUMLARAÑ         after the disaster. The project consists of three components
KARÎ¿ÑHAZ¿RL¿KL¿ÑOLUNMAS¿ÑVEÑACILÑDURUMÑM~DAHALEÑKAPASITESININÑ       complementing one another: preparing for emergencies in the
ART¿R¿LMAS¿ÑOKULLARÑVEÑHASTANELERÑGIBIÑyNCELIKLIÑKAMUÑBINALAR¿N¿NÑ   aftermath of earthquakes through risk mitigation measures on
G~lLENDIRILEREKÑVEVEYAÑYENIDENÑYAP¿LARAKÑDEPREMÑRISKININÑ            individual, family and institutional levels and enhancing
AZALT¿LMAS¿ÑIMARÑVEÑYAP¿ÑMEVZUAT¿ÑAl¿S¿NDANÑBELEDIYELERINÑ           emergency preparedness capacity, mitigating seismic risks on
KURUMSALÑVEÑTEKNIKÑKAPASITELERININÑART¿R¿LMAS¿ÑlAL¿ÎMALAR¿ÑGIBIÑ      high priority public buildings (schools, hospitals and other public
BIRBIRINIÑTAMAMLAYANÑ~lÑBILEÎENDENÑOLUÎUYOR                          buildings) by reinforcement and/or reconstructing , finally
                                                                      increasing the institutional and technical capacity with regard
                                                                      to building codes enforcement at the municipalities.

Istanbul Disaster Response Plan

                          TAMP                                The Istanbul Disaster Response Plan (TAMP) was prepared.
                                                             Within TAMP Istanbul; there are 106 agencies and
                          Ë34!."5,                          institutions employing 330 thousand people under
                                                           26 service groups of 4 services.




3AFEÑ,IFEÑ4RAININGÑANDÑ#OMMUNICATIONÑ#AMPAIGN


      826,552 people were trained with the awareness raising                  3AFEÑ,IFEÑÑÑ
        activities. 235 thousand Istanbul residents became the
         3AFEÑ,IFEÑ6OLUNTEERSÑ!LMOSTÑÑMILLIONÑMATERIALSÑWEREÑ
             shared with Istanbul community within the training
                                                                               Trainings
                                     and communication activities.




                                                                              Designed as a part of TAMP Istanbul, the project made the
                           )STANBULÑ3AFEÑ,IFE                                stakeholder analysis for 450 agencies and institutions for
                                                                            establishing a volunteering model that will take part in all the
                         Volunteers System                                 phases of disaster management. The disaster management and
                                                                          volunteering systems of 5 countries were also analyzed and as a
                                                                         result, a strategy and action plan was prepared and put in place.




    With the project, it was aimed to establish a system that will
  enable the evaluation and accreditation of volunteers according
                                                                         Volunteer
     to their updated information and competences. 13 workshops
      were held with institutions and NGOs; 123 voluntary function
                                                                          Accreditation
      areas were developed. Procedures were determined and a pilot
   implementation process began for the accreditation of volunteers.

                                                             1175
       Reinforcement and
       Reconstructing Projects

                                           944                       944 school buildings were either reinforced or
                                                                    reconstructed within the ISMEP project. Thus,
                                                                   school buildings with an area of almost 3 million
                                                                  square meters became earthquake resistant.




 More than 1.5 million students started to study in safer
    buildings. With the reinforcement and reconstructing         Safe
  projects, the indoor spaces of schools were raised by 2.5
     times; the number of classrooms by 1.8 times; and the
                           number of students by 1.7 times.
                                                                  Buildings



                                                 74
                                                                               74 hospitals and/or polyclinics
                                                                              were made earthquake resistant
                                                                             within ISMEP.




4 of the most important hospitals of Istanbul, with an area
of almost 1 million square meters, namely Göztepe Training

      and Umraniye Maternity and Pediatrics Hospital are being
       demolished and reconstructed. After the construction, it is
                     targeted to serve 5.5 million people per year.




                                    LEED Gold                             The hospitals which are designed with the
                                                                         “Seismic Isolation System” to serve continuously

                                   Certificate
                                                                        even in the case of an earthquake will the first
                                                                       public hospitals in Turkey to be a candidate for
                                                                      the LEED Gold Certificates.




   Within the project, 1175 public buildings
     including the other administrative ones
      were either reinforced or reconstructed.

Environment Friendly
and Innovative Design

   With the architectural revisions, energy saving in
  hospitals and schools raised by 40%. A decrease of
                                                                Energy
          25% in water consumption and 35% in gas
                           consumption were achieved.            Efficiency
